## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
  [*] --> Idle
  Idle --> QueryIntersections: request /intersections
  QueryIntersections --> ReturnIDs: if response type = IDs
  QueryIntersections --> ReturnDetails: if response type = FullDetails
  ReturnIDs --> Idle
  ReturnDetails --> Idle
  Idle --> WatchState: request /watch
  WatchState --> Watched: on success
  WatchState --> ErrorWatch: on 400/403
  Watched --> Idle
  Idle --> UnwatchState: request /unwatch
  UnwatchState --> Unwatched: on success
  UnwatchState --> ErrorUnwatch: on 400/403
  Unwatched --> Idle
```
